          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer35607157">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10896055110945934702">Table For Two proves a delectable gormandizing experience with two light-hearted Harlequin romance from Nora Roberts topped with her vast knowledge of Italian and French haute cuisine as a garnish. <br /><br />Summer Desserts, the first story is about the fiercely independent French chef Summer Lyndon finding herself attracted to smarmy and suave hotelier Blake Cochran. Love conflicts with Summer's career and causes an avalanche of control issues in a dramatic high. <br /><br />The more enjoyable fare turns out to be L</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText10896055110945934702">Table For Two proves a delectable gormandizing experience with two light-hearted Harlequin romance from Nora Roberts topped with her vast knowledge of Italian and French haute cuisine as a garnish. <br /><br />Summer Desserts, the first story is about the fiercely independent French chef Summer Lyndon finding herself attracted to smarmy and suave hotelier Blake Cochran. Love conflicts with Summer's career and causes an avalanche of control issues in a dramatic high. <br /><br />The more enjoyable fare turns out to be Lessons Learned when notorious skirt-chaser Carlo Franconi unwittingly surrenders to Juliet Trent, his publicist who finds a heart behind his devastating facade. It is fluffy romance with a dose of humor and fairy-tale charm. The insecurities of Juliet and his reputation as a playboy proves disastrous for their fragile trust. <br /><br />What makes this book irresistible is Ms. Roberts's flair, delicious male protagonists and sumptuous descriptions of the dishes, which makes it a nice indulgent treat for romance fans.</span>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer79677005">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10339988027437573208">I have mostly read Fiction from Nora Roberts and was concerned these stories were listed as romance. Much to my surprise and delight, this was not what I would consider trashy romance, but more fiction with a great romance. They didn't really seem much different than most of her fiction work, and I loved them just as much. <br /><br />I am a big fan of french cooking, and believe I also enjoyed the main characters being chefs. Nora delights me again and again. Never a bad story by this great author.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5403616915560368034">A light read. Both books are rather old so the people smoke indoors, take knives and oils on airplanes, professional persons have to use payphones but if you can see pass that you have a soft and sweet summer read.<br /><br />Both books are rather predictable and I found book 2, Lessons learned, more so. The hero, an Italian chef, was the fantasy of a Mediterranean male with his romance and lively hands but still, a good read for a lazy afternoon when you dont want to use your brain.</span>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review" id="review_782852402">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/782852402" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/21008693-pupottina" class="left imgcol" title="Pupottina"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1378965677p2/21008693.jpg" alt="Pupottina" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/782852402?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Dec 16, 2013</a>

      <a href="/user/show/21008693-pupottina" class="user" title="Pupottina">Pupottina</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it">really liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/18775781-cupcakes-a-colazione" title="ebook 9788858917329" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a href="/review/list/21008693-pupottina?shelf=romance" class="actionLinkLite">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer782852402">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7177302123684013848">Ingrediente essenziale: l’amore, anche in cucina.<br /><br />Nora Roberts riesce sempre ad intrattenere con stile e raffinatezza. Di questo libro, che intenerisce, fa sognare l’anima e il palato e riempie di gustosi sapori l’esistenza, cambierei soltanto il titolo, CUPCAKES A COLAZIONE, ritenendo più idoneo quello originale “Table for two”, ossia “Tavolo per due”. Infatti, sono due le storie racchiuse nel volume, edito da Harlequin Mondadori, e due sono i protagonisti legati all’universo, sempre più in voga</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText7177302123684013848">Ingrediente essenziale: l’amore, anche in cucina.<br /><br />Nora Roberts riesce sempre ad intrattenere con stile e raffinatezza. Di questo libro, che intenerisce, fa sognare l’anima e il palato e riempie di gustosi sapori l’esistenza, cambierei soltanto il titolo, CUPCAKES A COLAZIONE, ritenendo più idoneo quello originale “Table for two”, ossia “Tavolo per due”. Infatti, sono due le storie racchiuse nel volume, edito da Harlequin Mondadori, e due sono i protagonisti legati all’universo, sempre più in voga, dell’arte della cucina e del dessert. Non soltanto fragranti e soffici cupcakes, ma prelibatezze da menù completo. Ogni portata è servita per soddisfare ogni palato o qualsiasi esigenza del cuore, per una clientela prettamente femminile.<br />In DOLCI INCONTRI, la chef Summer Lyndon, una bella donna con la mania del perfezionismo in ogni delizia che crea, viene ingaggiata dal seducente Blake Cochran per creare un menu prestigioso per il suo ristorante di lusso a Filadelfia e, tra attrazione reciproca e segreti di famiglia, l’amore sarà l’ingrediente principale. <br />In LEZIONI DI CUCINA, torna come protagonista maschile, Carlo Franconi, uno dei migliori chef italiani e personaggio secondario nel primo romanzo, racchiuso in questo volume di doppie emozioni. Prima era l’amico e confidente di Summer. Qui, è lo chef che ha da poco pubblicato il suo ultimo libro di ricette e sta per intraprendere un tour promozionale, insieme all’agente pubblicitaria Juliet Trent. Per lei, un lavoro è un lavoro e non è mai stata intenzionata ad intrecciare relazioni personali, quando c’è un rapporto professionale, ma con lo chef italiano Franconi, qualcosa non le fa rispettare i piani. Il merito del dolce tormento è la tecnica persuasiva di lui.<br />Per Summer e Carlo, in queste due storie romantiche, è il momento di trovare, e svelare alle lettrici della Roberts, qual è l’ingrediente giusto del “per sempre”: l’amore vero.<br />È una coppia di storie romantiche “da regalare” alle amiche e “da regalarsi” per concedersi un magico sogno d’amore.<br />Anche se la Roberts, che preferisco, è quella delle storie un po’ thriller e di suspense, i colpi di scena lei riesce ed inserirli anche qui, in una coppia di romanzi, dove sensualità, amore e ottima cucina si fondono insieme alla perfezione del suo stile e delle sue trame sempre appassionanti. <br /><br />“Il romanticismo va bene per i libri e i film.”<br />“Il romanticismo va bene dappertutto. Dovresti provare vino, lume di candela e musica a basso volume. Concediti l’esperienza. Non ti farà male!”<br /><br /><a rel="nofollow" href="http://youtu.be/Bw6lgn1gllA" target="_blank">http://youtu.be/Bw6lgn1gllA</a><br /></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/2905301?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Jul 13, 2007</a>

      <a href="/user/show/81564-sarah" class="user" title="Sarah">Sarah</a>

        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it">liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span></span>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">someone looking for summer mind-candy -- but well-written candy</span></div>

        


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a href="/review/list/81564-sarah?shelf=fiction" class="actionLinkLite">fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer2905301">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17250487015296119478">What I learned from this book:<br /><br />1) If you're a good writer, you can make even the worst cliches entertaining as hell. I can't stand trite romances, and yet Nora Roberts has me giggling and taking an extra half hour for lunch so I can finish my book.<br /><br />2) Reprints of novels written in the mid-eighties are amusing if only for the reminder of the days when one could take one's set of prized knives on an airplane (our Hero is a chef), takes one's own olive oil and vinegar on an airplane (our Hero is a ve</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText17250487015296119478">What I learned from this book:<br /><br />1) If you're a good writer, you can make even the worst cliches entertaining as hell. I can't stand trite romances, and yet Nora Roberts has me giggling and taking an extra half hour for lunch so I can finish my book.<br /><br />2) Reprints of novels written in the mid-eighties are amusing if only for the reminder of the days when one could take one's set of prized knives on an airplane (our Hero is a chef), takes one's own olive oil and vinegar on an airplane (our Hero is a very picky chef), but one could also take one's lighter on the plane in anticipation of lighting up upon reaching cruising altitude.<br /><br />3) I need to take a half dozen NR's with me and go sit on a beach for a week. Wanna come along?</span>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review" id="review_72256122">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/72256122" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/949924-maria" class="left imgcol" title="Maria"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1242245373p2/949924.jpg" alt="Maria" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/72256122?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Sep 25, 2009</a>

      <a href="/user/show/949924-maria" class="user" title="Maria">Maria</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it">really liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/248635.Table_For_Two" title="Mass Market Paperback 9780373285426" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a href="/review/list/949924-maria?shelf=romance" class="actionLinkLite">romance</a>, 
              <a href="/review/list/949924-maria?shelf=nora-roberts-re-reads" class="actionLinkLite">nora-roberts-re-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer72256122">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5802689872566003323">Both books, written about food, the cooking and eating thereof, are delightful. Originally published separately in 1985 and 1986, they both demonstrate the finer points of Ms. Roberts writing style. There is little if no suspense but the emotions and issues the characters deal with are believable and provide the tension the reader has come to look for from Ms. Roberts. Also, I am coming to appreciate more and more the absence of the one-line paragraph that so many authors are succumbing to these</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText5802689872566003323">Both books, written about food, the cooking and eating thereof, are delightful. Originally published separately in 1985 and 1986, they both demonstrate the finer points of Ms. Roberts writing style. There is little if no suspense but the emotions and issues the characters deal with are believable and provide the tension the reader has come to look for from Ms. Roberts. Also, I am coming to appreciate more and more the absence of the one-line paragraph that so many authors are succumbing to these days. Is this an editing or a writing problem? That is the question.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="5802689872566003323">...more</a>

          </span>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review nosyndicate" id="review_1192412228">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1192412228" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/23096635-maura" class="left imgcol" title="Maura"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1449144636p2/23096635.jpg" alt="Maura" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/1192412228?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Feb 06, 2015</a>

      <a href="/user/show/23096635-maura" class="user" title="Maura">Maura</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was ok">it was ok</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/248635.Table_For_Two" title="Mass Market Paperback 9780373285426" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a href="/review/list/23096635-maura?shelf=contemporary-romance" class="actionLinkLite">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a href="/review/list/23096635-maura?shelf=annoying-characters" class="actionLinkLite">annoying-characters</a>, 
              <a href="/review/list/23096635-maura?shelf=rakish-hero" class="actionLinkLite">rakish-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a onclick="Effect.toggle('reviewTextContainer1192412228'); return false;" href="#">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span style="display:none" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer1192412228">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12446957979432760349">Summer Desserts - 2/5 - The plot had some promise, but the failure IMHO was in the characters. Blake was wealthy, arrogant and demanding - but he wasn't all that bad really. The heroine is the one I hated. She grew up wealthy and demands the best of everything. She's vain and conceited. She knows she's the best dessert chef out there and doesn't show an ounce of modesty at any time. She's beyond arrogant and demanding when it comes to her profession. And am I supposed to find it charming and her</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText12446957979432760349">Summer Desserts - 2/5 - The plot had some promise, but the failure IMHO was in the characters. Blake was wealthy, arrogant and demanding - but he wasn't all that bad really. The heroine is the one I hated. She grew up wealthy and demands the best of everything. She's vain and conceited. She knows she's the best dessert chef out there and doesn't show an ounce of modesty at any time. She's beyond arrogant and demanding when it comes to her profession. And am I supposed to find it charming and her more likable because she enjoys junk food? It doesn't exactly add any depth to her character... At one point she calls another chef a peasant. Really? After the hero has told her to come to his office she thinks, "No one summoned her immediately. People requested her, at her leisure." So evidently the world revolves around the heroine. And this goes for the romance too...she has to be in control of it. It's a lot of lust, but not very romantic. Maybe I could have enjoyed this a bit more if the heroine hadn't been so arrogant...or if both of the characters didn't seem so shallow. <br /><br />Lessons Learned - 3/5 - This was a fairly decent story and I would have rated this higher if it weren't for the hero. He just did not appeal to me and I found myself getting irritated while reading. Juliet is the publicist assigned to celebrity chef Carlo Franconi's publicity tour of the U.S. He sex on legs and Juliet is rather repressed and completely commitment phobic. She starts out trying to keep a distance and maintain a professional demeanor. He steamrolls over all of her objections. <br /><br />My problem with Carlo is his ego. There's a fine line between confidence and arrogance and he's on the side of arrogance. Any man receiving a compliment who says, "Yes, I know." instead of "Thank you." is an arrogant ass. There is even a quote in the book, <em>"His ego was no small matter."</em> and it's not used as a euphemism. As a publicist, her job and her image is important to her, so making a public display of a relationship is a reasonable complaint...but Carlo doesn't care, because he wants what he wants (and don't even get me started on his childish little tantrum over ingredients - is that supposed to be endearing?). On top of that, the man is a flirt - he's slept his way around the globe and he flirts with anything on legs. So I'd be a bit wary about getting into a relationship with a man who loves women as much as he does. <br /><br />The heroine I actually liked. Her hesitancy to get involved seriously is all very realistic considering his reputation, the fact that they live on separate continents, etc. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span style="display: none" class="spoilerContainer">[Not to mention how he bungled the whole proposal thing...I mean, asking a woman to marry you after she's told you she hates what the marital state does to a woman and how she never wants to be in that position...not so smart.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><!--["br"]--><!--["br"]--><!--["br"]--><!--["br"]--><!--["br"]--><!--["br"]--></span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="12446957979432760349">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer6236099567769717173">This is two books in one and I would have rated it higher if they hadnt been so very very alike. I enjoyed the writing and the characters and separately would probably have liked them more. I understand that the characters overlap, but to my mind putting the two together is a mistake, as the plots and characters are practically identical. This does tend to come with the genre to an extent, but it's far too obvious here.<br />V Easy reading though, light and steamy, finished both in 24 hours.</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText6236099567769717173">This is two books in one and I would have rated it higher if they hadn´t been so very very alike. I enjoyed the writing and the characters and separately would probably have liked them more. I understand that the characters overlap, but to my mind putting the two together is a mistake, as the plots and characters are practically identical. This does tend to come with the genre to an extent, but it's far too obvious here.<br />V Easy reading though, light and steamy, finished both in 24 hours.</span>

  <a href="/user/show/18264031-reginlaradiosa" class="left imgcol" title="ReginLaRadiosa"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1420484880p2/18264031.jpg" alt="ReginLaRadiosa" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/842221186?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Feb 09, 2014</a>

      <a href="/user/show/18264031-reginlaradiosa" class="user" title="ReginLaRadiosa">ReginLaRadiosa</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it">really liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/19210010-cupcakes-a-colazione" title="Paperback 9788861834132" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer842221186">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11042299263709875001">Recensione presente sul sito <a rel="nofollow" href="http://www.reginlaradiosa.it" target="_blank">www.reginlaradiosa.it:</a> <br /><br />“Il romanticismo va bene per i libri e i film.” <br />“Il romanticismo va bene dappertutto. Dovresti provare vino, lume di candela e musica a basso volume. Concediti l’esperienza. Non ti farà male!”<br /><br /><br /><br />Il libro racchiude due romanzi brevi pubblicati molto tempo fa con la collana Harmony: “Dolci incontri” e “Lezioni di cucina”.<br /><br />Nel primo racconto la protagonista è Summer Lyndon, una famosa pasticcera che riceve una proposta di lavoro da Blake Cochran, sexy</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText11042299263709875001">Recensione presente sul sito <a rel="nofollow" href="http://www.reginlaradiosa.it" target="_blank">www.reginlaradiosa.it:</a> <br /><br />“Il romanticismo va bene per i libri e i film.” <br />“Il romanticismo va bene dappertutto. Dovresti provare vino, lume di candela e musica a basso volume. Concediti l’esperienza. Non ti farà male!”<br /><br /><br /><br />Il libro racchiude due romanzi brevi pubblicati molto tempo fa con la collana Harmony: “Dolci incontri” e “Lezioni di cucina”.<br /><br />Nel primo racconto la protagonista è Summer Lyndon, una famosa pasticcera che riceve una proposta di lavoro da Blake Cochran, sexy titolare di una catena alberghiera in continua espansione.<br /><br />Summer non è propensa ad accettare l’offerta di Blake e lui dovrà ricorrere a tutte le sue arti seduttive per riuscire ad assumerla. Il suo corteggiamento però va oltre l’ambito lavorativo e presto i due protagonisti non potranno fare a meno di ammettere ciò che provano.<br /><br />Il protagonista del secondo racconto è il cuoco italiano Carlo Franconi. L’acclamato chef ha pubblicato un libro di cucina e per il suo tuor promozionale viene affiancato dalla seriosa agente letteraria Juliet Trent.<br /><br />Carlo rimane subito affascinato dalla sua agente e tenta in tutti i modi di rompere quel muro di serietà dietro qui si nasconde la vera Juliet. Ben presto il grande Carlo Franconi deve arrendersi all’evidenza: è irrimediabilmente innamorato e farà di tutto per conquistare la donna della sua vita.<br /><br />Le due storie sono collegate dalla profonda amicizia che lega Summer e Carlo e da un mistero familiare..<br /><br /><br /><br />La narrazione è in terza persona, lo stile è scorrevole, semplice e accattivante. Nora Roberts, autrice da quattrocento milioni di copie, colpisce ancora.<br /><br />Per quanto i protagonisti siano ambiziosi, pronti a tutto per il loro successo dovranno soccombere alla forza dell’amore: l’autrice con questo fa capire che in amore non esistono ricette perfette, ogni gesto è diverso, ogni sentimento è particolare e il rischio è ciò che ci permette di arrivare alla felicità.<br /><br />Non sono sicuramente i due racconti migliori di Nora Roberts, ma io li ho apprezzati molto! Sicuramente il mio giudizio è influenzato dalla precendente lettura della prima edizione: averli di nuovo tra le mie mani, anche se in una nuova veste grafica, mi ha riportato a vecchi ricordi e al piacere di quella appassionante lettura.<br /><br />Questo libro è un mix di seduzione tra i fornelli, amore e ricette che lasciano un dolce sapore.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="11042299263709875001">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer3572974967152664082">A famous dessert chef gets the contract to design a new menu for a hotel and falls for the CEO. In the second story, a straight-laced publicist learns about love from an Italian chef while on tour with his new book. <br /><br />Paperback format only Reprint of two early romances: Summer Desserts and Lessons Learned. Light, easy-to-read romance. Recommended. </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer1326141474">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18034553469542401868">la force d'un regard<br /><br />Raconté d'un point de vue omniscient avec une alternance entre un focus sur l'héroïne et un autre sur le héros.<br /><br />Blake ne cherche pas forcément le grand amour ais il n'y est pas opposé pour autant. Au contraire de Summer qui fuit les relations amoureuses surtout quand celles-ci ont des allures de sérieux ! Sa carrière est sa seule priorité.<br /><br />Ils vont vite se retrouver dépasser par les événements car leur histoire n'a rien d'une petit amourette passagère ni d'une aventure sans len</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText18034553469542401868">la force d'un regard<br /><br />Raconté d'un point de vue omniscient avec une alternance entre un focus sur l'héroïne et un autre sur le héros.<br /><br />Blake ne cherche pas forcément le grand amour ais il n'y est pas opposé pour autant. Au contraire de Summer qui fuit les relations amoureuses surtout quand celles-ci ont des allures de sérieux ! Sa carrière est sa seule priorité.<br /><br />Ils vont vite se retrouver dépasser par les événements car leur histoire n'a rien d'une petit amourette passagère ni d'une aventure sans lendemain. Au contraire, il s'agit bel et bien d'au coup de foudre.<br /><br />La romance est racontée sous fond d'intrigue culinaire puisque Summer doit remettre à niveau le restaurant d'un des hôtel de BlaKe. Or, tout ceci se fait sous l'égérie de l'art et de la créativité ce qui se traduit pas un style notamment dans les descriptions culinaires particulièrement enlevé et imagé jouant sur les différent sens.<br /><br />un dénouement sans surprise vers lequel le lecteur est tranquillement amené au fil de l'histoire.<br />Une romance légère qui nous prend dans son tourbillon !<br /><br />Envoûtante Passion<br /><br />Nous restons dans l'univers culinaire avec cette deuxième romance dans laquelle nous retrouvons Carlo Franconi, personnage rencontré dans l'histoire précédente.<br /><br />Cette seconde histoire est placé sous le signe de l'humour et de la légèreté avec un héro typiquement charmeur comme on présuppose qu'on le sont tous les italiens et une héroïne, américaine, qui s'est jurée de ne surtout pas tombé sous son charme !<br /><br />Il s'agit d'une romance entre deux protagonistes que tout oppose mais en reprenant plus ou moins les mêmes ingrédients que l'histoire précédente. Peut-être, est-ce, en partie la raison pour laquelle le lecteur parvint plus difficilement à s'attacher à ces deux personnages et surtout à partager pleinement leur histoire.<br /><br />Lors du dénouement, le lecteur a plaisir à retrouver le personnage de Summer le temps de quelques pages.<br /><br />Une seconde intrigue dans la lignée de la première.<br /><br />Un diptyque drôle, sensuel pour un très bon moment de détente !</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="18034553469542401868">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer5651794842583989636">"Summer sentì la realtà allontanarsi da lei, ma non aveva alcun desiderio di fermarla.Avrebbe provato tutto ciò che doveva provare, sarebbe andata ovunque dovesse andare, purché Blake fosse con lei."<br /><br />Ogni tanto mi viene voglia di leggere qualcosa a tema "culinario" e questo libro della bravissima Roberts ha centrato in pieno lo scopo, una lettura decisamente "gustosa" e romantica! ;D Dalla sinossi pensavo che le storie di Carlo e Summer fossero contemporanee e invece i due amici si spartiscono eq</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText5651794842583989636">"Summer sentì la realtà allontanarsi da lei, ma non aveva alcun desiderio di fermarla.Avrebbe provato tutto ciò che doveva provare, sarebbe andata ovunque dovesse andare, purché Blake fosse con lei."<br /><br />Ogni tanto mi viene voglia di leggere qualcosa a tema "culinario" e questo libro della bravissima Roberts ha centrato in pieno lo scopo, una lettura decisamente "gustosa" e romantica! ;D Dalla sinossi pensavo che le storie di Carlo e Summer fossero contemporanee e invece i due amici si spartiscono equamente il libro a metà XD La prima parte è dedicata alla determinata Summer, migliore chef pasticcere del mondo, che si incontrerà, o meglio scontrerà, con l'affascinante Blake che per lei farà un'eccezione sulle relazioni sul posto di lavoro XD La sfida tra i due è accesa tanto sul piano lavorativo quanto su quello personale, Blake rimane subito affascinato dalle mille sfumature di quella talentuosa ragazza che cucina i dolci più sublimi per lavoro e divora hamburger e pizza nel privato ed è ben determinato ad averla nella sua vita...per sempre. Ovviamente non sarà facile, Summer ha ricevuto dai genitori tanto affetto ma anche tanti esempi di amore passeggero e bastano le due magiche paroline a farla scappare a gambe levate XD La seconda metà è dedicata a Carlo invece, uno dei suoi migliori amici, uno chef italiano con i fiocchi che ama tanto la pasta quanto le donne, che si susseguono veloci ma con cui riesce sempre a rimanere in ottimi rapporti (è stato educato da una famiglia di donne del resto! chi le capisce meglio di lui? XD). Troverà pane per i suoi denti nella sua nuova agente pubblicitaria, Juliet, che crede che il cibo sia una mera necessità (scandalizzando il nostro chef) e l'amore viene decisamente al secondo posto rispetto al lavoro; nel breve viaggio promozionale la sua corazza di ghiaccio si scioglierà ma per infilarle un'anello al dito ci vorrà ben più di un piatto di pasta...ci vorrà un elefante ahahah XD</span>

        <a href="/review/show/398709607?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Aug 23, 2012</a>

      <a href="/user/show/9125314-dalimar" class="user" title="Dalimar">Dalimar</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it">liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer398709607">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer580344024270026948">Solo lei la primera parte de esta serie de dos.Summer Dessert.Bueno en este libro tenemos a Summer,que es una pastry chef,super reconocida.Pero es mas terca que una mula.Demaciado obstinada.No cree para nada en el amor,ya que su mama que es una reconocida actriz,se ha casado innumerable cantidad de veces siempre sonando con el amor verdadero.Su papa le sigue los pasos a su mama en cuestiones de bodas.Debido a esto Summer no soporta la idea del amor y mucho menos la del matrimonio.Eso la impulsa</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText580344024270026948">Solo lei la primera parte de esta serie de dos.Summer Dessert.Bueno en este libro tenemos a Summer,que es una pastry chef,super reconocida.Pero es mas terca que una mula.Demaciado obstinada.No cree para nada en el amor,ya que su mama que es una reconocida actriz,se ha casado innumerable cantidad de veces siempre sonando con el amor verdadero.Su papa le sigue los pasos a su mama en cuestiones de bodas.Debido a esto Summer no soporta la idea del amor y mucho menos la del matrimonio.Eso la impulsa mas hacia su carrera y a seguir logrando mas éxito profesional.En ocasiones su personaje caía en lo frívolo y egocéntrico,de hecho no lo encontré muy definido.Tal vez Nora Roberts lo creo así para dar a entender el porque ella rechaza tanto el amor.<br /><br />En el personaje masculino tenemos a Blake,que dirige el imperio familiar pero el hotel en Filadelfia se ha quedado rezagado por lo que le pide los servicios a Summer para que lo ayude a mejorar su carta en el restaurante del hotel.Lo curioso es que cada uno tenia sus ideas pre concebidas sobre ellos.Ella lo cree el típico ejecutivo,calvo,gordo y con traje de diseñador y el piensa que ella esta pasada de peso debido a tener que probar todo tipo de dulces y también piensa que es una señora de mediana edad con harina en la cara.Lo que hace que les sorprenda el hecho que ella es una chica muy guapa y el un hombre guapisimo y encantador.Lo que hace que ella rechace su propuesta,pues debido a su rechazo hacia el amor no quiere ser tentada bajo los encantos y el magnetismo sexual de Blake.Pero este se las ingenia para persuadirla y que acepte trabajar en su restaurante.<br /><br />Les cuento que al principio al menos su 25 primeras paginas era super y desesperantemente aburrido.De hecho esas primeras paginas me tomo 2 días en leerlas pues no quería retomar la lectura,pero al final mi curiosidad pudo mas y seguí leyendo.El libro no me ha encantado,pero luego del comienzo tan fatal,puedo decir que fue mejorando y llego a ser un libro pasable.Todo gracias al personaje de Blake,que el el hombre que todas queremos guapo,millonario,cariñoso,amable,atento y muy enamorado.Y por poco lo olvido sin las ocurrencias de Monique la madre de Summer,un personaje encantador que como dato curioso fue amante del padre de Blake,cuando este pasaba por una crisis matrimonial.<br /><br />Leere el segundo a ver que me parece....</span>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review" id="review_430870008">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/430870008" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/3023796-julie-barrett" class="left imgcol" title="Julie Barrett"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1378144888p2/3023796.jpg" alt="Julie Barrett" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/430870008?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Oct 09, 2012</a>

      <a href="/user/show/3023796-julie-barrett" class="user" title="Julie Barrett">Julie Barrett</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it">really liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/248635.Table_For_Two" title="Mass Market Paperback 9780373285426" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer430870008">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15402447819191491911">Table for Two by Nora Roberts<br />two books about chefs and romance in one.<br />Summer Desserts<br />Dessert chef Summer Linden falls in love with the owner Blake Coccoron, family owned hotels all over the world. He's got a proposition for her baking.<br />Perfection-she won't take anything but. It took her 3 hours to make that treat and she was used to doing that, traveling to make special treats for special high priced people.<br />He presented her with a challenge and then told her who he'd hire if she refused: an enemy</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText15402447819191491911">Table for Two by Nora Roberts<br />two books about chefs and romance in one.<br />Summer Desserts<br />Dessert chef Summer Linden falls in love with the owner Blake Coccoron, family owned hotels all over the world. He's got a proposition for her baking.<br />Perfection-she won't take anything but. It took her 3 hours to make that treat and she was used to doing that, traveling to make special treats for special high priced people.<br />He presented her with a challenge and then told her who he'd hire if she refused: an enemy of hers.<br />Lots of hot steamy sex along with the baking and organizational skills make this an excellent read.<br />When she gets injured her mother is around to help take care of her and that is driving her up the wall.<br />.<br />Lessons Learned<br />Carlo Franconi is in love with her, the publicist. Juliet <br />Love the shopping trip in the middle of the night.<br />He's trying to make a meal from fresh ingredients and everything is going wrong. The wrong ingredients, they are not fresh and the table isn't going to<br />be strong enough. He is promoting his book by traveling to big cities and giving a demo of Italian pasta.<br />He indulges her when preparing her a meal when they don't have any promo plans for the rest of the day. Love all the travel and sounds as hectic as it was for them.<br />Hot steamy sex combined with the food makes this a great read.<br />Recipes included!<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5060581866979210368">"Summer Desserts" was...meh. <br />But, "Lessons Learned" was superb. I was hooked from page one &amp; finished the book in only a few hours. I couldn't put it down. I would recommend this book. </span>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked &amp;&amp; exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked

    }
  }

    <div class=" clearFloats bigBox" id="aboutAuthor"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/625.Nora_Roberts">About Nora Roberts</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
      <a href="/author/show/625.Nora_Roberts"><img alt="625" src="http://d.gr-assets.com/authors/1440685355p2/625.jpg" class="right" /></a>
    <div class="readable">
      
<span id="freeTextContainer3894340981613935157">Nora Roberts was born in Silver Spring, Maryland. She began writing when a blizzard in February 1979 kept her in her hilltop home with a three and six year old for nearly a week of canceled kindergarten and dwindling chocolate supplies. <br /><br />During the now-famous blizzard, she pulled out a pencil and notebook and began to write a story for her own entertainment. From the first page, she knew it was wha</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText3894340981613935157">Nora Roberts was born in Silver Spring, Maryland. She began writing when a blizzard in February 1979 kept her in her hilltop home with a three and six year old for nearly a week of canceled kindergarten and dwindling chocolate supplies. <br /><br />During the now-famous blizzard, she pulled out a pencil and notebook and began to write a story for her own entertainment. From the first page, she knew it was what she was meant to do. Several manuscripts and rejections later, Irish Thoroughbred was published by Silhouette in 1981.<br /><br />The Liar, published in April 2015 by Putnam, is her 214th book. She hit the NY Times Bestseller list in 1991. Every book since 1999 has made that list.<br /><br />Recently The New Yorker called her “America’s favorite novelist."<br /><br />In 1995, she began writing a police procedural series featuring Eve Dallas, a NY homicide cop, and set in the near future under the J.D. Robb pseudonym. Devoted in Death, out in September 2015, is the 41st entry in the series.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="3894340981613935157">...more</a>

    </div>
    <a href="/author/show/625.Nora_Roberts" class="actionLink moreLink">More about Nora Roberts...</a>
